>
> **[2:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=146)** Our revenue is still consistent with the number of requests, but our costs are a little bit more unpredictable.
>
> **[2:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=152)** We have a higher fixed cost at $50 per month, but we scale better as the number of requests increases.
>
> **[2:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=158)** Our margin will get better the more and more requests that we handle.
>
> **[2:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=162)** But in the lower request range, we'll have a lower margin and potentially a negative margin.
>
> **[2:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=167)** So the drawback of this approach is its often hard to predict margins 'cause we need to know how many requests we're going to have, and in this case, it's hard to predict margins because it's often really difficult to time model scalability for a continuous use case.
>
> **[3:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=182)** So using the same prices will have different costs, whether we're using a third party model with unit pricing or running our own.
>
> **[3:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=190)** But for our end customer, they don't care.
>
> **[3:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=192)** We are presenting the same kind of pricing so they get the same experience.
>
> **[3:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=196)** So what are the benefits of unit pricing?
>
> **[3:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=198)** The first benefit is that it's simple for a customer to understand.
>
> **[3:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=202)** They send you some information, you bill them for that amount.
>
> **[3:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=205)** The second benefit is that it's consumption based revenue.
>
> **[3:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=208)** So the more that your users use, the more you earn.
>
> **[3:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=211)** The third benefit is it's easy to predict margin or cost depending on what kind of model you're using.
>
> **[3:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=217)** The fourth benefit is that this is a great type of pricing when integrating with third party APIs.
>
> **[3:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=223)** You just attach a fixed margin and away you go.
>
> **[3:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=226)** Now the fifth benefit or drawback is you can compete or lose on market price.
>
> **[3:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=232)** In some cases, like right now, some AI products are actually being priced under cost, so it might be very difficult to generate the revenue that you need at unit pricing.
>
> **[4:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=242)** In the next video, we'll talk about a variant of unit pricing, which is based on time.
>
> **[4:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/unit-and-margin-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=247)** We'll talk about consumption time-based pricing.

#### Time consumption pricing for AI
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] Many people get paid by the hour.
>
> **[0:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=2)** So can we price AI in the same way?
>
> **[0:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=5)** The answer is yes, with time-based pricing.
>
> **[0:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=8)** We've seen this already in the course.
>
> **[0:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=10)** It's quite common in the cloud world and we've seen it for GPU based pricing.
>
> **[0:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=14)** As an example, here's a screenshot for the pricing of GCP GPUs per hour.
>
> **[0:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=20)** Now we can apply the same technique for pricing for our own customer.
>
> **[0:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=24)** So let's go through a case study.
>
> **[0:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=26)** Our use case is that we're doing document entity extraction, where users submit jobs and get their information back.
>
> **[0:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=32)** So this is going to be asynchronous.
>
> **[0:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=35)** So going into our key information, we'll assume that it takes around one minute to process a page per document.
>
> **[0:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=42)** Cost to our business is $0.50 per hour and we're going to price it for $5 an hour for our customer.
>
> **[0:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=49)** So this gives us a gross margin of around 90%.
>
> **[0:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=52)** And because this is an asynchronous workload, we can have elastically scaled resources, meaning that our graph looks very similar to the unit based pricing that we saw with a third party vendor.
>
> **[1:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=64)** Now, similar to our previous base pricing, we can always adjust our margin based on the market price.
>
> **[1:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=70)** Now, at this use case, we assume that we have zero time to actually spin up and spin down any hardware, and in practice this isn't true.
>
> **[1:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=78)** So we might want to add in a minimum time consumption charge.
>
> **[1:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=82)** So looking at a similar table, if we look at the bottom, we can see that the startup time per document is one minute to spin up the GPUs, CPUs, and process the data.
>
> **[1:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=92)** So in that case, we might charge a minimum increment of one minute.
>
> **[1:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=96)** If the customer is submitting tiny little documents, maybe just a sentence long, we won't be reducing our margin.
>
> **[1:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=103)** What are the benefits of time consumption pricing?
>
> **[1:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=106)** They're easy for customers to understand.
>
> **[1:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=108)** They're similar to cloud-based costs, where you're charged by the amount of time it takes for a task to complete.
>
> **[1:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=114)** Now, this might be harder for a customer to forecast, but this is common for the whole cloud industry.
>
> **[1:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=119)** And the next benefit is that we're mimicking the pricing of cloud resources.
>
> **[2:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=123)** So as a result, it's easier to calculate our margin.
>
> **[2:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=126)** The third benefit is that if we optimize our throughput, we can actually improve our margins.
>
> **[2:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=131)** On the other side, if we optimize the speed of our processing, we might actually decrease margins.
>
> **[2:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=137)** So there's a little bit of complexity here on how this billing actually works.
>
> **[2:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/time-consumption-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=142)** In the next video, we're going to talk about value-based pricing and how we can frame the pricing discussion outside of our costs.

#### Value-based pricing for AI
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] If someone offered to trade $1 for $10, would it be too good to be true?
>
> **[0:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=6)** Well, that's the goal of value-based pricing, to sell a solution that's cheaper than what someone is currently paying.
>
> **[0:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=13)** In the context of AI, many companies are selling automation for existing processes, such as writing documents, extracting information, and automating call centers.
>
> **[0:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=23)** Many companies allocate costs for these tasks, like pricing a support ticket at $10 across a support system.
>
> **[0:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=30)** In other words, that company might value a sold support ticket at $10.
>
> **[0:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=36)** So as a support automation company, you might charge $1 per ticket.
>
> **[0:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=41)** Now, for the company buying the solution, that's a clear win.
>
> **[0:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=44)** They're getting $10 worth of value for just $1, but how do you measure this value?
>
> **[0:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=49)** There can be some challenges.
>
> **[0:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=51)** First challenge is it's hard to measure when value is attained.
>
> **[0:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=55)** For example, with the support ticket, does this value come from a ticket being closed, or does the customer need to be satisfied?
>
> **[1:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=62)** And going even deeper, is it possible to be satisfied in a situation where a customer is asking for support?
>
> **[1:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=68)** So understanding the business process is very important to understanding the value that you're delivering.
>
> **[1:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=74)** Another challenge is that value may be long term.
>
> **[1:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=77)** For example, in the search engine optimization space, you could use AI generated content, but search engine optimization takes time, so even though you might generate hundreds or thousands of articles, there might be downstream effects on brand, engagement and overall marketing impact.
>
> **[1:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=94)** So you might be in a situation where you've sold immediate savings, but caused long-term harm to a customer.
>
> **[1:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=100)** So as a vendor, it's very important to understand the value to the customer.
>
> **[1:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=105)** So let's go through an example.
>
> **[1:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=106)** Earlier on, we were pricing our sentiment classifier, and the cost to our business is 50 cents per thousand reviews.
>
> **[1:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=113)** Now, the customer might value this at $500 per thousand reviews.
>
> **[1:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=118)** That might be the current benefit to the business, or the current cost they pay for manual labeling.
>
> **[2:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=123)** So as a company, your value proposition might be, we'll label a thousand reviews for you for $50, so you save 90% of the cost and from our perspective, we're only paying 50 cents per thousand reviews, so we get a markup of over 9900%, or a margin of 99%.
>
> **[2:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=143)** That's pretty good.
>
> **[2:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=144)** So in positioning value-based pricing, take the perspective of your customer.
>
> **[2:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=148)** I can help you reduce your cost by 90%.
>
> **[2:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=151)** That's a very compelling sales pitch.
>
> **[2:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=153)** Now in practice, you'll need to make sure that you can validate that number with case studies or other metrics and to summarize value-based pricing, it's an easy sell.
>
> **[2:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=163)** You can clearly communicate the value you're providing to your customer versus an alternative.
>
> **[2:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=168)** This makes it very easy for your customer to say yes.
>
> **[2:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=172)** They no longer have to build an internal business case.
>
> **[2:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=174)** You've done it for them.
>
> **[2:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=175)** Now, the challenges are it's hard to measure.
>
> **[2:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=178)** You need strong data to back up these claims, whether through metrics or through case studies.
>
> **[3:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/value-based-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=184)** In the next video, we'll cover our fourth type of pricing, which is subscription-based pricing.

#### Subscription pricing for AI
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] In this video, we'll cover subscription-based pricing.
>
> **[0:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=4)** This is a common technique in the software world, giving rise to the industry of SaaS.
>
> **[0:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=9)** Now, the benefits of subscription-based pricing is that it offers predictable revenue.
>
> **[0:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=13)** An example of subscription-based pricing is that ChatGPT costs $20 us per month for the premium subscription and to the average user ChatGPT's pricing is pretty simple, but there also exists a teams and enterprise plan.
>
> **[0:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=27)** This is similar to the other SaaS services that we've seen, for example, weights and biases from our training chapter.
>
> **[0:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=34)** Now, for many existing businesses like Microsoft, Salesforce and Google AI is a common add-on.
>

>

>
> **[1:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=67)** Now, the challenge with SaaS based pricing is that it can be challenging to estimate cost.
>
> **[1:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=71)** For example, with ChatGPT, what if a user asks a thousand questions?

>
> **[1:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=79)** Well, this might be the case, one of the smart things that OpenAI has done is limit usage for GPT-4.
>
> **[1:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=86)** So you have unlimited usage for the cheaper 3.5 model, and you're limited as if this video's making to 40 messages for three hours for GPT-4.
>
> **[1:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=95)** The other item that's interesting is that most users follow a power law relationship.
>
> **[1:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=99)** With your top 10% of customers using the most amount of resources.
>
> **[1:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=104)** This number varies, it might be 80%, it might be 50, it might be 95.
>
> **[1:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=110)** But with smart pricing, it's possible to mitigate these expensive users.
>
> **[1:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=114)** Now, there are a few techniques you can use for mitigating costs and increasing revenue.
>
> **[1:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=118)** The first one might be to price for a healthy average margin, meaning that even though you have power users at the top end of your spectrum, you'll still be making a good margin for the average user.
>
> **[2:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=129)** The second technique is to limit consumption at the upper end, just how like OpenAI limits GPT-4 usage.
>
> **[2:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=135)** The third option is to have multiple subscription options.
>
> **[2:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=139)** This allows power users to self-select and upgrade to more powerful offerings.
>
> **[2:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=144)** And the fourth option is to include some kind of consumption-based pricing where users can top up and buy additional credits of some form to utilize the services they need.
>
> **[2:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=154)** A good example of this is Zapier's based pricing.
>
> **[2:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=157)** Let's take a look on their website.
>
> **[2:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=159)** As we can see here, we have the standard pricing for various types of plans.
>
> **[2:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=164)** As a power user, if I need to automate more tasks, I can see my pricing.
>
> **[2:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=168)** At a certain number of tasks, I can no longer subscribe to the starter plan.
>
> **[2:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=173)** You can also see that my pricing has gone up based on this consumption.
>
> **[2:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=177)** Now, with the different techniques that we've learned, we can combine them to form our pricing strategy.
>
> **[3:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=181)** At the company I work at, which is Voiceflow, we combine SaaS-based pricing for every user that utilizes the product, consumption-based pricing for the number of interactions that you have with your assistant and unit based pricing for AI generative tokens.
>
> **[3:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=198)** So through this model, we try to mitigate costs and capture upside.
>
> **[3:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=202)** Now, an important consideration for subscription-based pricing, are utilization metrics.
>
> **[3:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=208)** For example, if we have five users, we can see how they're each using our product.
>
> **[3:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=213)** For our margin, our goal is to have a target utilization rate.
>
> **[3:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=217)** Now, users two and three are hovering around our utilization metric goal, that's great.
>
> **[3:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=222)** Now, customers four and five, they have low usage.
>
> **[3:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=226)** This means that they're potentially a churn risk and we might not renew them in the next contract period.
>
> **[3:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=231)** To summarize subscription based pricing for AI, the benefits are that we can get predictable revenue.
>
> **[3:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=238)** It's also easy to cross sell AI for existing products.
>
> **[4:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=241)** We can also combine subscription-based pricing with other pricing to mitigate downside and get potential upside.
>
> **[4:08](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/subscription-pricing-for-ai?u=76281980&t=248)** And with subscription-based pricing, we need to measure utilization to avoid surprises with users leaving.
>

>
> **[0:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=51)** After a proposal is approved, the company receives funding but must provide monthly receipts and project updates to make sure that they're delivering.

>

>
> **[1:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=73)** Now, the next program type is for research.

>
> **[1:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=82)** One such funding program in Canada is called Mitacs.
>
> **[1:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=85)** In this program, companies provide a project and provide funding to hire a research intern.
>
> **[1:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=90)** The Mitacs organization, along with the government, contribute to this to create a research award.
>
> **[1:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=95)** This funding is awarded to a partner university which will help complete the project.
>
> **[1:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=100)** Another large program is a retroactive tax incentive.
>
> **[1:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=103)** In Canada, this program is called SR&ED.
>
> **[1:46](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=106)** SR&ED stands for Scientific Research & Experimental Development.
>
> **[1:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=109)** Once a company fills out a project, they can submit a claim to the government and receive tax credits for these innovative projects.
>
> **[1:57](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=117)** The government will then determine and provide a grant based on the submission.
>
> **[2:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=121)** The benefit of this program is you don't have to determine ahead of time which projects you'll work on.
>
> **[2:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=126)** Since the AI industry moves so quickly, it's easier to compile a report after the fact and submit it for government funding.
>
> **[2:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=132)** Now, the third type of funding is more bespoke.
>
> **[2:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=135)** If you're a large organization, the government and partner universities might work with you in both the funding and research capacity.
>
> **[2:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=142)** One of the examples in Canada is the Vector Institute, where a consortium of companies, the provincial government, and the federal government, came together to form an AI institute.
>
> **[2:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=153)** Now, with these different types of support programs, it's possible to de-risk your AI projects.
>
> **[2:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=158)** Many of these projects are designed to help companies compete against their larger peers, especially in the AI innovation space.
>
> **[2:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=165)** You should visit your government's website to see what kind of programs are available to you.
>
> **[2:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=170)** This types of funding is becoming increasingly more important as AI becomes a globalized phenomenon.
>
> **[2:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/start-up-funding-and-grant-programs-for-ai?u=76281980&t=175)** Now, in our next video, you're going to receive a challenge, taking all the skills you've gained about pricing and being challenged to price a logo generator.

#### Building a business case for AI projects
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] In this video we're going to cover creating an AI business case.
>
> **[0:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=4)** Now, this is the structure we're going to follow.
>
> **[0:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=6)** We're going to present a problem or opportunity, a solution, key metrics, a financial analysis, a resource ask, and the risks for this proposal.
>
> **[0:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=18)** Now, for the purpose of this video, we're going to focus on an e-commerce B2B software company.

> **[0:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=28)** An initial idea is that our digital support experience is not very good.

>
> **[1:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=75)** But for the next year, we have a flat budget for support.

>

>
> **[1:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=113)** For example, asking for a refund, using our order tracking software, understanding our reward point system, integrating with our return scheduler or our exchange based software.

>
> **[2:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=164)** Now, for each of these metrics, these are the numbers I'm assuming.
>
> **[2:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=168)** I'm assuming our bot support volume will go from 10% to 50%.
>
> **[2:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=172)** Our overall support volume will decrease.
>
> **[2:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=175)** Our customer satisfaction will increase from around 70% to 80%, that our churn rate will decrease due to better support.
>
> **[3:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=184)** Our time to response will be 50% lower.
>
> **[3:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=186)** Our time to resolution will be 30% lower, and our social media sentiment for digital assistance will be 10% higher on net promoter score.
>
> **[3:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=196)** And from a financial perspective, my projected ROI is to break even by nine months.
>
> **[3:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=202)** I'm projecting that our top line growth will be an extra 1% year over year due to our customer satisfaction improvements and our social media net promoter score.
>
> **[3:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=212)** This project will cost $250,000 for three months as a CapEx investment.
>
> **[3:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=218)** And from an OpEx perspective, we're going to spend $25,000 per month for bot improvements and maintenance.
>
> **[3:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=225)** We're also going to decrease our support OpEx due to fewer future support hires and our support center lowering our outsource volume.
>
> **[3:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=234)** So my ask is for $250,000, $100,000 for a new SaaS support platform, and 150,000 for two developers and one product manager for three months.
>
> **[4:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=246)** And these developers and product manager will continue to support this platform and replace that support OpEx we discussed earlier.
>
> **[4:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=253)** And from a risk perspective, we need to make sure that the platform provides correct answers.
>
> **[4:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=259)** We need to make sure that our hiring or upskilling efforts will be successful.
>
> **[4:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=264)** We also have a platform risk.
>
> **[4:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=265)** We need to make sure that the bot system that we're using is better than our previous one.
>
> **[4:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=271)** In the past, we found that the previous system was not extensible enough.
>
> **[4:35](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=275)** So we need to make sure that when building our integrations our bot building platform is very extensible.
>
> **[4:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=281)** Now that wraps up our business case.
>
> **[4:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=284)** We've covered our problem solution, key metrics, financial analysis, resourcing ask, and risks.
>
> **[4:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/building-a-business-case-for-ai-projects?u=76281980&t=291)** In the next video we'll dive deeper into that financial projection and understand how we came up with these figures.

#### Solution: Building an AI business case
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=0)** (lively music)
>
> **[0:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=5)** - [Instructor] Let's go into a sample solution for creating an AI business case.
>
> **[0:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=10)** I'm going to go ahead and pitch you on my solution.
>
> **[0:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=12)** Our customers struggle in launching to new markets.
>
> **[0:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=16)** After talking to 50% of our high intention users, they said that translating their site takes too long.
>
> **[0:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=24)** 25% of our total users want to expand into new language locales in the next three months.
>
> **[0:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=31)** Those who have have spent 20 hours and a thousand dollars on average to translate their website, but only 20% of those who expressed interest actually did due to an unclear path forward.
>
> **[0:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=43)** So, I'm proposing an auto translate solution.
>
> **[0:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=47)** This will be a subscription add-on using AI to translate a customer's website.
>
> **[0:51](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=51)** On top of the AI feature, we'll include a locale entering plan to help our customers feel more comfortable.
>
> **[0:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=58)** We'll also be launching a premium version for larger catalogs that includes expert translation.
>
> **[1:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=64)** Getting into the financials, we expect a payback of three months and projecting a $75,000 profit per month afterwards.
>
> **[1:13](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=73)** We're assuming that with this launch we'll get 5% extra revenue from our existing customers with a thousand users subscribing to this plan.
>
> **[1:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=82)** We're estimating around 100,000 of additional revenue.
>
> **[1:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=85)** From a CapEx perspective, we're estimating $250,000 for three months, and then from OpEx, 25,000, 10,000 a month for AI translation, 5,000 per month for human translation, and $10,000 allocated for bug fixes and small improvements.
>
> **[1:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=104)** We'll be implementing a value-based pricing with a basic and premium plan.
>
> **[1:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=109)** Our monthly fee for this add-on will be $99 for the basic plan and $599 for the premium plan.
>
> **[1:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=116)** We'll be using Google Translate; paying around $20 per 1 million characters.
>
> **[2:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=120)** An average E-commerce website for our smaller users will have around 500,000 characters leading to an initial cost of $10.
>
> **[2:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=129)** This gives us an initial margin of 90%.
>
> **[2:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=132)** Now, the premium side, the websites will be larger leading to an average initial AI cost of $40.
>
> **[2:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=138)** Since we're including human translation, we estimate this will cost around $200 leading to an initial average margin of 60%.
>
> **[2:27](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=147)** Now, we anticipate that the customers signing onto this plan are prime for launching into a new market.
>
> **[2:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=153)** Now, in every subsequent month, we assume that usage will be lower because customers won't be launching to new locales every month.
>
> **[2:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=159)** Continuing our financial analysis, we expect our lifetime customer value for this add-on to be around $198 for two months worth of subscription.
>
> **[2:50](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=170)** For a premium user, we're expecting $6,000 for 12 months worth of subscription.
>
> **[2:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=175)** We're expecting around a 30% churn per month on this add-on since customers may not be launching new products or expanding every month.
>
> **[3:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=183)** While the 30% churn is quite high, we still think that this will be a sticky plan and we hope to reduce that churn risk later on.
>
> **[3:10](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=190)** This is because customers will continue to add new products that require translation and growing stores will continue to expand.
>
> **[3:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=197)** And from a key metrics perspective, we'll be tracking a few.
>
> **[3:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=200)** The first one is the number of basic and premium add-ons.
>
> **[3:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=204)** The second is the number of translations done.
>
> **[3:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=206)** The third is the use of human expert translators.
>
> **[3:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=210)** The fourth is the percentage of translation that's done with expert humans and the amount that is changed.
>
> **[3:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=216)** The fifth is the churn number for these add-ons.
>
> **[3:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=220)** And the sixth is the number of customers expanding regionally.
>
> **[3:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=224)** With all these key metrics, we should be able to see if we're solving the customer problem.
>
> **[3:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=229)** Now, the ask for this feature is $250,000 over three months, we'll be hiring two developers, one front end and one backend, along with a product manager.
>
> **[3:59](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=239)** Now, the risks.
>
> **[4:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=241)** The main risk for this project is incorrect translations.
>
> **[4:04](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=244)** Another risk is post one month churn.
>
> **[4:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=247)** Having users who remove this add-on after doing their initial translation.
>
> **[4:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=251)** The third risk is having a lower margin, especially if we have high human translator needs.
>
> **[4:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=257)** The fourth risk is lower expansion than we anticipated.
>
> **[4:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=261)** And the fifth risk is higher usage of the AI feature due to a continuously changing product catalog that needs constant translation.
>
> **[4:29](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=269)** So overall, we think that we can help our customers launch to new markets by introducing a translation feature.
>
> **[4:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=276)** And there we go.
>
> **[4:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=277)** That's my pitch.
>
> **[4:38](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=278)** So hopefully you had an interesting experience developing a business plan for this E-commerce use case.
>
> **[4:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/solution-building-an-ai-business-case?u=76281980&t=284)** Now, in the next video, we're going to wrap up this course and crystallize everything that we've learned in the past number of videos.

### 8. ROI on AI Use Cases

#### ROI on AI customer support automation
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript
>
> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Narrator] Two years after the release of ChatGPT, we're all still wondering what has been the business ROI of gen AI?
>
> **[0:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=7)** In this chapter, we'll go through a few use cases and see what's emerged in the industry.
>
> **[0:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=12)** To start us off, we'll cover the ROI on AI customer support.
>
> **[0:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=16)** Now, customer support isn't homogenous.
>
> **[0:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=19)** There are actually different levels.
>
> **[0:21](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=21)** Depending on the complexity of a ticket, you classify them into different levels.
>
> **[0:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=26)** An example classification system I have here classifies tickets between L1 to L3.
>
> **[0:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=31)** With L1, being simple requests, L2, being a little bit more complex, and L3, requiring more technical knowledge.
>
> **[0:39](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=39)** Now, the reason I bring this up is that AI will handle different types of requests differently.
>
> **[0:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=44)** So, let's go into some case studies.
>

>
> **[0:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=58)** This was a pretty major announcement by a major company and showed the potential of AI in ROI.
>
> **[1:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=63)** We can scroll down through this article to find more specifics, including how many conversations were being done and the equivalent work of full-time agents.
>

>
> **[1:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=79)** For example, MavenAGI has a case study on the OpenAI website, discussing their ability to automate customer support.
>
> **[1:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=86)** As we scroll down, we can see an overview of the product and some metrics on average customer support costs and rates.
>
> **[1:34](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=94)** In this case, MavenAGI fine-tuned GPT-4 as part of their release.
>

>
> **[1:47](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=107)** You can see here we have a quick visualization indicating the rate of AI resolution week-over-week.
>
> **[1:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=113)** So we can see here there are a variety of published case studies on the effectiveness of AI customer support.
>
> **[2:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=120)** Now, while there are a number of different case studies, measuring ROI can actually be pretty complex.
>
> **[2:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=125)** There are different metrics used by customer support teams to figure out the ROI of these kinds of investments.
>
> **[2:11](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=131)** The first one is deflection, which measures how many requests did not go to a person, either in a contact center or asynchronously.
>
> **[2:18](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=138)** Meaning, how much did the AI deflect user questions.
>
> **[2:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=142)** Beyond deflection, there's also resolution, which is harder to measure.
>
> **[2:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=145)** This is how many tickets or tasks were completed with AI.
>
> **[2:30](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=150)** And finally, there's net promoter score.
>
> **[2:32](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=152)** Net promoter score measures the customer satisfaction on support tickets.
>
> **[2:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=156)** So figuring out how happy customers are with AI support and comparing that to humans.
>
> **[2:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=161)** Now, even with these three different metrics, every company and every support team measures them slightly differently, so there's no consensus of what the exact definition is of deflection or resolution.
>
> **[2:52](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=172)** Different agents on a team might also mark this with different levels of scrutiny.
>
> **[2:56](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=176)** Now, what's interesting is that with AI automation for customer support, pricing models are all a little bit different.
>
> **[3:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=182)** There are three typical models that we've seen and that we've talked about earlier in this course.
>
> **[3:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=187)** There's a SaaS pricing model, where you charge by seat, or a general subscription.
>
> **[3:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=192)** Consumption, which typically charges by the number of requests going to a customer system.
>
> **[3:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=197)** And by ticket, so measuring how many tickets get resolved by an AI system.
>
> **[3:23](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=203)** The per-ticket pricing is pretty interesting.
>
> **[3:25](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=205)** A number of companies are moving towards that, with the largest being Salesforce, which is charging $2 per conversation for its Agentforce model.
>
> **[3:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=213)** Again, this raises the question of what is an actual resolution?
>
> **[3:37](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=217)** Is a closed case when a customer is happy, or when they stop responding?
>
> **[3:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=221)** It gets a little bit philosophical and hard to measure.
>
> **[3:44](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=224)** Now, some recommendations for going into your AI projects for customer support.
>
> **[3:48](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=228)** So a few recommendations would be to audit your existing gaps and figure out where the limitations are in your existing system.
>
> **[3:55](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=235)** They could be an onboarding, documentation, complex systems.
>
> **[3:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=238)** There's really a variety of challenges in the customer support space.
>
> **[4:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=242)** Next, you need to figure out what kind of customer relationships you want to have.
>
> **[4:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=245)** Do you want AI automation for all your customers, or do you want to route them to human for more enterprise focused ones?
>
> **[4:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=252)** There's no right way to do this, and each business is different.
>
> **[4:15](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=255)** You should also examine the complexity of your tickets and your product.
>
> **[4:19](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=259)** AI resolution can work differently across different levels of complexity, as we saw with L1, L2 and L3 support.
>
> **[4:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=266)** You also need to make sure that you have good documentation, because AI systems rely on that to provide answers based on using different techniques, such as RAG.
>
> **[4:36](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=276)** You should also examine which support domains are actually taking the most amount of time, whether it's account related questions, pricing, product support, or more.
>
> **[4:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=285)** AI systems will be able to help differently with each of these different areas.
>
> **[4:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=289)** And finally, you should audit about your onboarding speed.
>
> **[4:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=293)** So beyond just existing gaps, onboarding speed for new employees of using these AI systems versus traditionally onboarding becomes quite important.
>
> **[5:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=302)** So overall, we've seen a huge potential in the ROI of AI customer support.
>
> **[5:06](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-customer-support-automation?u=76281980&t=306)** There are actually hundreds of companies working on this problem, so as it continues to grow, we'll see even more case studies come out.

#### ROI on AI lead generation

#### ROI on AI Copilots
> [LinkedIn Learning](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980)

> [!transcript]- Transcript

> **[0:00](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=0)** - [Instructor] In this video, we'll cover the general concept of AI copilots and their ROI.
>
> **[0:05](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=5)** Copilots come in three different flavors, general copilots that can help you with day-to-day tasks and aren't particularly specialized.
>
> **[0:14](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=14)** Then there are domain-specific copilots that might help in areas that have specific nuances, for example, sales or customer support.
>
> **[0:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=22)** There are also custom copilots that could be built for company-specific processes that need even more customization.
>
> **[0:28](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=28)** Now, depending on the task that you're trying to achieve, the results may vary.

> **[1:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=93)** Now, these numbers will largely vary and becomes challenging to actually assess which tasks have a high ROI and which ones have a low ROI.
>
> **[1:40](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=100)** Now, to examine this, let's look at a research paper.
>
> **[1:43](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=103)** "Navigating the Jagged Technological Frontier" is a great overview paper that covers where AI automation presents a high ROI versus where the quality decreases with the use of GenAI.
>
> **[1:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=114)** If we go down to page 31, we can see the concept that's provided in the paper.
>
> **[1:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=118)** It's called the jagged frontier of AI capabilities.
>
> **[2:01](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=121)** Jagged frontier demonstrates that on certain tasks, GenAI outperforms people versus on others it underperforms.
>
> **[2:09](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=129)** For example, in this chart, we can see that GPT outperforms a control group of people working on a specific task that's inside the frontier.
>
> **[2:16](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=136)** And we can see a further breakdown on page 35 where we can see that people who are very skilled at a task or less skilled at a task benefit from GenAI in different ways.
>
> **[2:26](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=146)** Now, in other tasks, like on page 37, we can see that GenAI can actually worsen the performance of somebody performing a task.
>
> **[2:33](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=153)** This is something that's outside the jagged frontier, meaning that GenAI and GenAI copilots still don't help people achieve a task better.
>
> **[2:41](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=161)** Now, scrolling up to page 33, we can see that there are a number of tasks that were studied.
>
> **[2:45](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=165)** I recommend you read this whole paper to get a better understanding on how AI automation can help people perform different kinds of tasks.
>
> **[2:53](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=173)** Now, we've been talking about productivity in a vague sense, but what does it actually mean to be productive?
>
> **[2:58](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=178)** Is being able to send emails more productive, or are we just creating more busy work for people?
>
> **[3:03](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=183)** This is a fundamental question that we'll learn as GenAI continues to evolve.
>
> **[3:07](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=187)** Now, when choosing to use AI copilots, we should take some considerations into account.
>
> **[3:12](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=192)** We should audit the work that's being done to make sure that we're delivering the highest value work at the right time.
>
> **[3:17](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=197)** We should also understand the current barriers to perform certain tasks.
>
> **[3:20](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=200)** For some barriers, GenAI can help.
>
> **[3:22](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=202)** For others, it might be a detractor.
>
> **[3:24](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=204)** We also need systems to verify the correctness of GenAI 'cause we don't want hallucinations to make it through the quality assurance process.
>
> **[3:31](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=211)** We should also think about how decisions are being made, whether AI automation is the one that's making the decision, or it's informing people with additional information and insights to make better decisions.
>
> **[3:42](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=222)** And finally, based on the concept of jagged frontiers, we should choose appropriate tasks for AI automation and copilots.
>
> **[3:49](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=229)** We want to make sure that we're choosing the right task to get the highest ROI.
>
> **[3:54](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=234)** So overall, the ROI on AI copilots is quite immense, ranging from general ones to domain-specific ones, to company proprietary ones.
>
> **[4:02](https://www.linkedin.com/learning/ai-pricing-and-roi-a-technical-breakdown/roi-on-ai-copilots?u=76281980&t=242)** And as AI copilots continue to evolve, I recommend that you test and experiment with them to figure out where the ROI is yourself.
